Overseas Chinese Refugees from Korea Arrive in Qingdao One After Another 63

▲A Total of More Than 2,600 People in Recent Days

A dispatch from Qingdao: Overseas Chinese refugees from Korea have returned to China and passed through Qingdao one after another. From the 15th to the 19th, there have been more than 2,000 people. The municipal chamber of commerce and social bureau have tried to accommodate them and sent them back to their hometowns one after another. Yesterday (21st) and today (22nd), two more batches have arrived, totaling more than 600 people. The ones who arrived in Qingdao yesterday were on the Guangli, a ship of the Zhengji Shipping Company, from Andong. They entered the port at 8:00 a.m., totaling 329 men and women. They also carried documents with the seals of the Andong County Government, the Andong Commercial Port Public Security Bureau, and the Andong Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating that thousands of refugees who had fled to Andong had reached. In addition to trying to accommodate them and raise funds for relief, there are now 329 refugees from Shandong Province, including 22 children, who are taking the Guangli ship of the Zhengji Company to Qingdao to go ashore and return to their hometowns. The ship is purely voluntary and provides free transportation. It is jointly certified to facilitate customs clearance when arriving in Qingdao and presenting it to the customs. After the refugees landed, the Public Security Bureau registered them by name, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Social Bureau sent people to accommodate them. At the same time, they contacted the Shipping Association for ships. On the day they sailed to Shijiusuo, there were only the Tongxing and Qingxing ships. However, the Tongxing was fully loaded and could not accommodate them. Therefore, only the Qingxing loaded 67 refugees and sailed to Shijiusuo that night to land. The rest were temporarily accommodated in the New Stage. This morning, 42 people took the Jiaoji Railway west. This afternoon, at 6:00 p.m., the Shipping Association prepared the Anshun and Zhaoxiang ships to carry 176 people to Shijiusuo. The rest who had no home to return to went to relatives and friends nearby. Just after this batch of refugees was sent away, another batch of refugees arrived in the afternoon. It is heard that they came to Qingdao from Yantai on the 16th Kyodo Maru, totaling 270 men, women, old and young. After landing, the Public Security Bureau, the Social Bureau, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent people to take care of them. A small portion, about 50 people, went directly from the Dagang Wharf to the Xiaogang Wharf to take the ships prepared by the Shipping Association and loaded them with those who came to Qingdao yesterday to return to their hometowns. The majority of more than 200 people, mostly from Qingzhou and Shouguang, needed to take the train west. It was too late to do so on the day and they were still accommodated in the New Stage. It is heard that the Social Bureau and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce have contacted the Jiaoji Railway Bureau for the refugees to take the train. The Railway Bureau has agreed to specially attach two third-class cars to the third train tomorrow to transport the refugees separately back to their hometowns (July 22).

Liaoning Various Legal Bodies Show Attitude Towards Korea 64

▲A Proclamation to the People of Japan and Korea: Since July 3rd, Koreans in various parts of Korea have gathered in crowds, attacking overseas Chinese. Some wielded weapons to surround and attack, others set fires everywhere, looting and destroying houses, and killing people. All kinds of atrocities were used to the extreme, resulting in the corpses of our defenseless compatriots piled up like pillows, their blood flowing. Those who were spared also lost their property and became displaced. The turmoil has expanded and intensified. As of today, it has been a week and there is no sign of it subsiding. The bad news has spread and people are shocked. Such a great tragedy in the world not only makes the Chinese people grieve, but also knowledgeable people in Japan and Korea, for the sake of humanity and diplomacy, should also harbor endless regret. The Chinese people believe that the cause of this disaster is absolutely incredible. According to newspaper reports, the Japanese authorities stated that "the direct cause was the Wanbaoshan Incident, and the fundamental cause was the accumulation of resentment from years of oppression of Korean farmers in Northeast China, which led to the current retaliatory act." However, the Chinese people find this explanation even more difficult to understand. The facts of the Wanbaoshan Incident were witnessed and heard by everyone. Unless deliberately confusing right and wrong, it cannot be said that the fault lies with China. The occurrence of this case was nothing more than someone, in the name of Korean farmers, renting land without legal procedures, cultivating it into rice paddies, diverting water by digging canals, building embankments, digging into the land of other Chinese farmers, and cutting off the navigation of the two counties. Those who were directly affected naturally had to rise up for legitimate self-defense. However, the Japanese authorities took military action, as if facing a formidable enemy. Chinese officials, deeply fearing the deterioration of the situation, tried their best to dissuade and suppress, and the Chinese farmers immediately swallowed their anger and left, quietly awaiting a solution, without any conflict with the Koreans. Not only were no Korean farmers killed or injured, but they are now continuing their construction work under the strict supervision of armed Japanese police. The attitude of the Chinese people is like this, how can they be repaid with revenge? This is one point. As for the claim that Northeast China has been oppressing Korean farmers for years, it is even more of a castle in the air, completely unfounded. The number of Korean farmers who have migrated to Northeast China has been increasing year by year, and has now reached more than a million. Although there are occasionally a small number of people who disrupt public order, the Chinese authorities cannot but crack down on them, but those who are law-abiding have never been subjected to any oppression. The continuous arrival of Korean farmers can be taken as an example. The Chinese authorities treat Korean farmers like this, so where does the resentment come from? This is the second point. As mentioned above, it can be seen that the indiscriminate killing and looting of overseas Chinese by Koreans in Korea seems to have other motives. Many people in the world say that some people are using ignorant crowds to instigate and direct them in order to achieve certain ambitions. The fabrication of news and sensationalism by various Japanese and Korean newspapers also have the suspicion of inciting and confusing. The Chinese people are reluctant to believe all these things, but clues can be found everywhere. Unless there is strong evidence to the contrary, it is difficult to dispel the suspicions of the Chinese people. Moreover, what the Chinese people find most painful is that, according to current international law, even in the event of formal war between two countries, non-combatants of the enemy or combatants who have lost their ability to resist must not be harmed. Now, overseas Chinese in Korea who are legally residing and peacefully earning a living, regardless of age or gender, are being killed indiscriminately for no reason. Even after fleeing, they cannot guarantee their lives. Regardless of the Wanbaoshan Incident, no Korean farmers were killed or injured. Even if there were, it is absolutely unacceptable to use such cruel means against innocent third parties. Disregarding justice and destroying humanity, it can be said that it has reached its limit. Japanese police are known throughout the world for their perfection and thoroughness. They have been able to quickly suppress any past incidents in Korea and restore stability. It is not known why this time they neither made sufficient preparations beforehand nor actively protected them afterward, allowing the overseas Chinese to suffer huge sacrifices and creating an unprecedented tragedy. Therefore, the Chinese people believe that even if the crime was entirely committed by the rioters themselves, the Japanese authorities, who failed to protect their residents in accordance with the treaty, must bear their due responsibility under international practice. It is hoped that there are many enlightened people in friendly countries who will seek to preserve the honor of their civilized and advanced countries. Next, please frankly state the true intentions of the Chinese people regarding the issue of Korean farmers' migration. All the disputes in the past regarding the migration of Korean farmers to Northeast China have stemmed from the issue of dual nationality. If Korean farmers are willing to naturalize and reside for a long time, China can also cooperate. However, after the Korean farmers naturalize, the Japanese authorities do not recognize Chinese nationality law, which leads to disputes from time to time, which in turn involve diplomacy and evolve into various ominous events. China has long hoped for a fundamental solution, but it awaits sincere consultation from the Japanese authorities. In short, the Wanbaoshan rice paddy incident and the Korean massacre in Korea are two completely different matters and cannot be discussed together. It must also be understood that all problems should be solved in a proper way in order to be effective. If all that is done is revenge, it will not only be useless, but also create obstacles, which is not wise. It is hoped that the people of Japan and Korea will pay close attention to the villains, not fall for their tricks, and strive to supervise the government and maintain international friendship. Then, the friendship between China and Japan, the overall situation in East Asia, and world peace will be fortunate. Sincerely, I offer this advice, and I hope you will take it into consideration. Liaoning Provincial National Diplomacy Association, Liaoning Provincial Education Association, Liaoning Provincial Farmers' Association, Liaoning Provincial General Chamber of Commerce Federation, Liaoning Federation of Trade Unions, Liaoning Press Federation, Liaoning Lawyers' Association, Liaoning National Common Sense Promotion Association, Fanyang City Chamber of Commerce, Shenyang City Education Association, Liaoning Youth Association, Liaoning Buddhist Association, respectfully.

▲Reply to the Statement from the Koreans: All colleagues of the Joint Council of Various Circles in Korea, your statement of July 8 has been received with respect. Our association sincerely accepts it. The Chinese and Korean nations not only have close historical, geographical, economic, and cultural ties, but also share the same environment of oppression and exploitation. We should maintain considerable friendship and abandon all doubts. The occurrence of this unfortunate incident is entirely due to incitement by a third party. The Chinese people have a very clear understanding of this and do not harbor any animosity towards the Koreans. In the Wanbaoshan case, the Korean farmers rented rice paddies without legal procedures, which cannot be considered valid. They forcibly dug a canal for twenty-five miles from Mashankou to Wanbaoshan, destroying crops and building a dam on the Yitong River. Farmers cannot but stop illegal infringement of their own interests, but their attitude was very peaceful and no conflict occurred, and there were no casualties. The Chinese anti-Korean reports in the Japanese and Korean newspapers are completely fabricated. On July 2, Chinese farmers filled in the ditch, and the Japanese police first opened fire. There were no casualties on either side. However, the Japanese took the opportunity to send armed military police with several machine guns, digging trenches, burying landmines, and forcibly occupying civilian houses. Such atrocities are unbearable for any nation. Moreover, they incited ignorant Koreans to riot and massacre innocent people, dismembering them and causing an unprecedented tragedy, which is the most heartbreaking thing. However, the Chinese people still have good feelings towards the Koreans living in Korea, and will listen to the government's negotiations with Japan and seek a fair judgment from the world. They will maintain a calm attitude and deal with it. It is hoped that your colleagues will sincerely announce the truth of the Wanbaoshan case and the attitude of the Chinese people towards the Koreans to the people in various parts of Korea, so as to avoid doubts, and not be used by third parties. It is further hoped that after this unfortunate incident, the feelings between the Chinese and Korean nations will become more harmonious. Respectfully replied by the Liaoning Provincial National Diplomacy Association.

▲Attached Translation of the Korean Statement: Representatives from all walks of life sincerely express their regret for the unfortunate incidents that occurred to the Chinese people in Incheon, Seoul, Pyongyang, and other places, triggered by the Wanbaoshan issue. They also declare that the occurrence of this unfortunate incident is definitely not due to the will of the entire Korean nation. They firmly believe that the Chinese and Korean nations, which have the closest relationship in history, geography, culture, and economy, are inevitably in a situation to maintain close friendship and support each other in the present and future. However, this accidental unfortunate incident can still enhance and attempt to be an opportunity to promote the sense of friendship between the two nations. We hope that the Chinese people will understand the true intentions of the Korean nation, and not remember this unfortunate incident. Furthermore, we ask that you abandon the doubts that have always alienated the millions of Korean compatriots in the East, and sweep away the factors that hinder the friendship between the two races, and resolve the issue of the Korean compatriots in the East with magnanimity and goodwill in a reasonable way. Finally, we once again regret that our most well-meaning neighbor suffered misfortune at the hands of our compatriots in our country. At the same time, we sincerely wish our good neighbors a speedy return to normalcy, to live in peace and enjoy a life of happiness and prosperity.

Zhu Mao's Remnant Bandits Invade Ruijin Again 65

▲The Western Fujian Militia Has Been Putting Up a Strong Defense

Shantou, 16th: The Jiangxi Communist bandits Zhu Mao and Peng Huang were attacked from both the left and right wings and could not take care of both ends. They fled towards the border of Fujian. A part of them reached Tingzhou. The city is flat on all sides and there is no natural defense, so the bandit army was able to enter directly. When the bandits arrived, all the shops closed their doors and the residents fled the city. The bandits extorted 10,000 yuan from the Chamber of Commerce. The Chamber of Commerce sent people to collect it everywhere, but only got 7,000 yuan. They were spared burning and killing that day. Local bandits and ruffians took the opportunity to agitate, claiming to overthrow local bullies and killing people in the market. No one dared to intervene. On the morning of the 10th, the bandits suddenly retreated towards Ruijin, Jiangxi, leaving a small part in Tingzhou. No one was in charge of the local area. Shops and houses were closed tightly, and thieves were rampant, searching every house. People were very panic-stricken. On the 15th, Luo Jieren, the commander of the joint security team of Shanghang, Tingzhou, Liancheng, and Yongding, sent He Jiqing to Shantou to ask Commander Zhang Ruigui for assistance with military pay and ammunition. According to He, Luo Jieren guarded the city of Shanghang with about 20,000 militiamen. Zhong Shaokui, Zhong Guanxun, Chen Rongguang, and Chen Shenfu's armed self-defense groups guarded the line from Wuping Fengshi to Yongding, also with about 2,000 people. Lu Xinming's bandit suppression army in Liancheng Qingliu Guihua also had an equal number. Recently, about 2,000 people from the Jiangxi militia led by Li Tianqi, Zhong Wencai, and Pan Manshan have been added to deploy defenses at the border of Wuping. At present, the local armed forces in western Fujian are no less than 7,000 to 8,000 people. It is said that the fleeing bandits in Tingzhou will be wiped out in one fell swoop.

10th: Zhu Mao's remnant troops fled from the Jiangxi border into Tingzhou and were pursued by the bandit suppression army. The main force then retreated back to Ruijin, Jiangxi, leaving only a small part and the fake propaganda team stationed near Changting. Luo Jieren, the commander of the Tinghang Lianyong security team, heard the news and immediately stepped up defenses, transferring the Jiangxi militia led by Zhong Wencai, Li Tianqi, and Pan Manshan to Wuping as reserves, vowing to defend their hometowns with all their strength. Defense works were built at Fengshi Nanshedu Zhongdu (the junction of Shanghang and Yongding), and Zhong Shaokui, Zhong Guanxun, Chen Rongguang, Chen Shenfu, and Chen Delong were assigned to defend them. The militiamen were all brave and good at fighting, and there were heavy troops stationed in the rear areas of Dapu and Yongding on the Fujian-Guangdong border, so the momentum was very strong.

Counterfeit Military Supply Bond Case Discovered in Guangdong Province 66

▲The Printing Company Has Been Sealed

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Guangdong Finance Authority recently issued 10 million yuan of second military supply bonds. The printing of the bond paper has always been done locally. This time, a tender was opened for printing, and the China Printing Company in the city won the bid with the lowest price. Therefore, the second batch of military bonds was all printed by the company. Since the start of printing, the Finance Department has sent personnel to the company every day to supervise the printing. The procedure was very solemn. The Finance Department has also issued the printed bonds one after another to various agencies and groups for distribution. However, after the bonds were sold, a certain store discovered that the seal of the Finance Department on the bond it recognized was slightly smaller. The store immediately telegraphed the Finance Department for inquiries. The Finance Department immediately retrieved the bond for detailed review and realized that the printing and paper of the bond were not different at all. The only slight difference was the size of the seal of the Finance Department. Therefore, it was determined that there must be a counterfeit military bond agency outside. Without making a sound, people were secretly sent to investigate. It was later found that the source of the counterfeit bonds came from the China Printing Company, which printed the real bonds. Personnel were immediately sent to the police to surround and search the company at Gongri Gate in the city. The company's manager, He Naihui, and the toolmaker, Lu Mianchu, were detained and taken to the Finance Department for strict interrogation. At the same time, the four supervisors who were sent out that day, Tao Houpei, Zhai Lan, Ke Lihui, Zhong and He Shiqing, were also detained and questioned. According to the Finance Department, the printing company had three suspicious points: (1) The seal of the Finance Department's supervisor on July 6 was still wet on July 15th at noon. (2) Multiple books of intact counterfeit bonds were found in the company's warehouse, and their numbers were not far from the numbers of the counterfeit bonds in circulation. (3) The company's printing plates were inspected, and the 100-yuan and 50-yuan plates were missing. Based on the above suspicious points, the Finance Department sent its staff Li Deyu, Lin Shuwen, Liang Qingzhu, Zhao Leifu, and Li Weizhi, along with four special agents and several policemen from the Chentang Branch, to seal the printing factory at 1:00 pm on the 16th. The criminals will also be convicted during the day. As for the number of counterfeit bonds that have been sold on the market, the exact number is still unknown to the outside world. (July 17)

Liaoning Province's Plan for the Reform of Police Administration 68

▲Division into Twelve Public Security Zones

Shenyang Correspondence: Huang Xiansheng, the director of the Liaoning Provincial Police Department, has been determined to rectify the police administration of the entire province since taking office. Recently, after following Deputy Commander Zhang to Beijing, he took the opportunity to inspect the police administration in various places. He felt that the police administration in the capital was the most complete, so he expressed to people that Liaoning Province, which connects the north and south, should emulate the capital for rectification. He immediately drafted a reform plan, submitted it to Deputy Commander Zhang in Beijing for approval, and then started with zoning after returning to Liaoning. The entire province was divided into twelve public security zones, and a captain was assigned to each public security zone to command it. Liaoning Province has a total of 104 public security infantry companies, with 10,606 police officers; 66 cavalry companies, with 3,113 police officers; 20 artillery companies, with 1,568 police officers; 21 independent cavalry platoons, with 514 police officers; and 34 independent artillery platoons, with 1,354 police officers. In total, there are 27,157 police officers. Depending on the complexity of the affairs in each district, the above number of police officers will be allocated in appropriate proportions. The drafted plan has been submitted to the provincial government for review and approval. Chairman Zang Shiyi considered the proposed plan to be well-considered, but since it involved changes to the public security team system, it must be sent to Chen Wenxue, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, for review and then ordered to be implemented to show prudence. It has already been submitted to the Department for review yesterday. The content of the zoning plan proposed by the Provincial Police Department is recorded below. The first zone (Shenyang, Liaoyang, Liaozhong, Fushun, Benxi) is commanded by Zhang Fengxi, with eleven infantry companies, three cavalry companies, two artillery companies, one independent cavalry platoon, and two independent artillery platoons. The second zone (Heishan, Beizhen, Panshan, Tai'an) is commanded by Liu Weihan, with five infantry companies, three cavalry companies, one artillery company, two independent cavalry platoons, and three independent artillery platoons. The third zone (Jin County, Suizhong, Xingcheng, Jinxi, Yixian) is commanded by Gong Wenchao, with nine infantry companies, three cavalry companies, one artillery company, two independent cavalry platoons, and four independent artillery platoons. The fourth zone (Gaiping, Haicheng, Yingkou, Fuxian) is commanded by Zhou Yuwen, with eight infantry companies, two cavalry companies, one artillery company, one independent cavalry platoon, and three independent artillery platoons. The fifth zone (Fengcheng, Andong, Xiuyan, Zhuanghe, Kuandian) is commanded by Zhang Yishan, with ten infantry companies, no cavalry companies, one artillery company, two independent cavalry platoons, and four independent artillery platoons. The sixth zone (Huanren, Xinbin, Jian, Tonghua) is commanded by Zhang Zongzhou, with thirteen infantry companies, one cavalry company, three artillery companies, two independent cavalry platoons, and one independent artillery platoon. The seventh zone (Tieling, Qingyuan, Kaiyuan, Xi'an) is commanded by Yao Jiayu, with sixteen infantry companies, four cavalry companies, three artillery companies, two independent cavalry platoons, and two independent artillery platoons. The eighth zone (Hailong, Liuhe, Huinan, Jinchuan, Dongfeng) is commanded by Qiao Weiqing, with eighteen infantry companies, five cavalry companies, two artillery companies, four independent cavalry platoons, and no independent artillery platoons. The ninth zone (Linjiang, Changbai, Antu, Fusong) is commanded by Yu Rongfa, with twelve infantry companies, no cavalry companies, ten artillery companies, no independent cavalry platoons, and one independent artillery platoon. The tenth zone (Faku, Changtu, Yingwu, Xinmin, Kangping) is commanded by Zheng Kuiwu, with four infantry companies, fourteen cavalry companies, two artillery companies, no independent cavalry platoons, and three independent artillery platoons. The eleventh zone (Liaoyuan, Huaihe, Tongliao, Lishu, Bianyi Mountain) is commanded by Fu Duolin, with no infantry companies, eighteen cavalry companies, three artillery companies, four independent cavalry platoons, and one independent artillery platoon. The twelfth zone (Taonan, Zhanshu, Kaitong, Tao'an, Zhendong, Tuquan, An Guang) is commanded by Song Liansheng, with no infantry companies, thirteen cavalry companies, no artillery companies, one independent cavalry platoon, and seven independent artillery platoons. (July 18)

Recent News on the Xu Min Dyke Protection Case 69

▲Provincial Government Sends Personnel to Xuzhou for Investigation

▲The People Propose Three Measures

Xuzhou Correspondence: After the Xu Bu dyke protection incident occurred, the local communities held a meeting on the aftermath of the June 30th Massacre to reach a temporary solution. After the case was reported to the provincial government, the provincial office sent Fu Zhiren to Xuzhou for investigation. The people living on the former Yellow River dyke heard the news and gathered in a team on the afternoon of the 22nd to petition Fu, with about two to three hundred people. The flags were marked as the Yuanqiao Township People's Dyke Protection Petition Group. The group members each held a small flag. Hu Rongqing, who died in the case, his sons Hu Zhensheng, Hu Desheng, Hu Xiaosan, and their families also participated in mourning clothes. The representatives Liu Gongchen and Shufan presented three conditions to Fu: (1) Jiudetang illegally bought more than twelve hectares of official dykes. Please cancel the contract for Jiudetang to buy the dyke and investigate the person in charge of Jiudetang. (2) Zuo Shuyi, the Director of the Bureau of Official Assets, colluded with Jiudetang and caused the tragedy. Please dismiss and punish him. (3) Yang Wei, the magistrate of Tongshan County, did not investigate the facts, arrested the people and imprisoned them, and opened fire to injure people. Please investigate him. Fu replied that he had investigated all parties, and expressed the following regarding the three matters requested by the people: (1) Jiudetang did have a license issued by the Ministry of Finance, but did not have a license issued by the county government, which is suspicious. The circumference of the city has a high embankment of more than twelve hectares, and the price for each acre is one yuan and five jiao, totaling more than one thousand eight hundred yuan. The sale of official assets in various places has never been so cheap, which is the second suspicious point. Jiudetang undertook the work during the tenure of Li Enbao, the former director of the Bureau of Official Assets, and the documents were vague and unclear, with no boundaries in all directions, which is the third suspicious point. This will have to wait for the county government to investigate and deal with it. (2) The truth about the case handled by the current Director of the Bureau of Official Assets, Zuo Shuyi, has been investigated and will be dealt with appropriately after being reported to the province. (3) The county government should not have beaten the people to death, which has also been investigated, but the county government also has a corresponding theory, which also needs to be reported to the province for review and approval. Finally, the people asked the province to distinguish between priorities and allow the people to undertake the official dyke according to Jiudetang's purchase price, and hand over the documents and photos to be submitted to the province. Only then did they disperse. (July 22)

Jiangsu Construction Department Convenes Construction Meeting 71

▲Discussion of the Construction Plan for the 20th Year

The Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, with the commencement of the 20th year, urgently needs to determine its construction policy for implementation. In the past, construction project plans in various counties were based on the county as a unit. Due to differing levels of affluence and varied terrains, all construction projects often lacked mutual coordination and adjustment, hindering overall development. Therefore, construction officials from various counties are being summoned in batches to the provincial capital for meetings to discuss everything. In addition to the mandatory attendance of one secretary from the Construction Department, the chief of the First Section, and the chief of the Second Section, directors of construction bureaus and technicians from construction offices in each county should attend the meetings in batches according to the scheduled dates. The scope of the meeting includes: 1. Construction officials from each county reporting on the work done in the previous year, achievements in recruiting labor for road construction, the status of bridges, culverts, and road surface progress; 2. Reporting and discussing various construction project plans for the current year, discussing methods for organizing the various construction-related economic incomes of each county, reporting on the types of construction taxes and levies, the actual amount collected compared to the targeted amount, and the amount of funds held and accumulated by the construction bureaus of each county; 3. Reporting on the budget for construction expenditures in each county for the current year and the administrative status. Matters concerning water conservancy, highways, and electricity can be addressed by having the chairman request the director of the department to temporarily designate the responsible personnel for those matters to attend. All proposals, after being approved by the attendees, will be submitted to the department for adoption and implementation. The meeting dates are from August 5th to August 25th, with meetings held in batches.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 73

Pseudo-Group etc. Escorting Song Xun to be Tried - Zhang Tongsheng, the pseudo-leader of the Lake Bandit Taibao A Shu's group, nicknamed Gaojiao Pai Siquan, has been captured by the water police in Wuxi. After obtaining a confession, a squad of police officers was dispatched today (the 24th) to escort the bandits Zhang Tongsheng and Miao Aye to Songjiang for trial by the bandit suppression headquarters. Zhang is tall and robust with a swarthy complexion, and one can tell at a glance that he is a man of strength. Zhang demanded to ride in a rickshaw to the headquarters, while Miao followed behind on foot. According to Zhang's confession to the water police, he said that recently, due to the urgent arrests by the military and police, he fled to the countryside of Wuxi, to a fish pond area to avoid capture. He suffered greatly and ran out of money. He had been constantly on edge and restless. He borrowed accommodation in a small inn and couldn't sleep all night. He went to a small teahouse for tea early in the morning to wash his face and was arrested before he finished, suggesting that these bandits were reaping what they had sown.

Songsi Road Project Submitted to Department for Review - The foundation of the Song-Wei county road in this county was previously partially constructed. The work of raising the road surface is also nearing completion, but continuous rain has inevitably caused some erosion. The director of the Construction Bureau, Mr. Sun Shengzeng, has hired workers to raise each section. There are also twelve bridges and nine culverts on the Songsi Road. The planned drawings, estimated expenses, etc., have been prepared and submitted to the department for review and approval, and a public tender will be announced soon.

Suzhou 74

Various Industries Resolve to Sever Economic Relations with Japan - The County Chamber of Commerce convened a meeting of representatives from various industries on the 24th, and resolved: (1) The transportation industry representative reported that starting from today, the transportation of Japanese goods would be stopped. (6) A general meeting will be held on the afternoon of the 26th to elect committee members.

Tourists at Garden Hotel Commit Double Suicide by Poison - In room 41 of the Garden Hotel at Sibaidu outside the city gate, tourists Gao Xixiong and Chen Yunfeng, a man and a woman, simultaneously ingested opium to commit suicide on the 23rd. After being discovered by the waiter, they were sent to Suyong Hospital for treatment. Because they had ingested a large dose of poison, Gao Xixiong died at 1 a.m. on the 24th, and Chen Yunfeng died at 4 a.m. The local prosecutor's office was notified to send personnel to investigate. Gao Xixiong was from Suzhou, and his father, Gao Bomei, has prepared a coffin to collect the body. Chen Yunfeng was from Changzhou and her family is being awaited to arrive in Suzhou before arranging for burial.

Continuous Rain Causes Disaster, Ferry Services Suspended - Recent continuous rain has caused the low-lying areas of Suxiang Nanbeiqiao Xishan Hengjing and other villages to become swamps. Farmers are complaining endlessly. In the urban area, the water has risen several inches above the banks along the city wall outside Xumen and at the Shantang Bazibao Bridge. All ferry services in the villages have been completely suspended. A section of the city wall at the Shuiguan Gate of Lao Chanmen collapsed for over ten *zhang* on the 24th, injuring one person. Reports of collapsing houses occur several times a day in various places.

Chuansha 75

Theft Case Cracked - On January 29th of this year, the houses of farmer Chen Yiyun in Yangjiazhai South in the Fifth District, and Zhang Liankui outside the East Gate in the First District, were robbed of property worth approximately over one thousand silver dollars. The victims reported the case to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. On the 18th of this month, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, Zhu Jusun, acting on a tip from an informant, ordered the police to proceed to Lao Jiang, under the jurisdiction of Nanhui County, and arrested the four suspects in the case: Huang Zishan, Chen Xiaodi, Chen Niubao, and Shi Xiaohua. Under interrogation, they confessed to robbing the Chen and Yang families' properties. They were handed over to the county government on the 22nd for trial.

Nanhui 76

Strictly Prohibit Fraud in Purchasing Cotton on Credit - Some citizens, including Cai Jinxiu, have stated that it is a custom in the countryside of this county that every autumn harvest, some people purchase cotton from farmers on credit, promising payment later. People often trust these verbal agreements, and there are no written contracts. As a result, some unscrupulous individuals take the cotton but do not pay promptly, delaying payment and even resorting to lawsuits. Judges often rule against the creditors because they have no evidence, and farmers suffer greatly. The autumn harvest is approaching, and it is important to take preventive measures. Therefore, a petition has been submitted to the county government requesting a prohibition, and the county government has issued a notice to all farmers, urging them to carefully consider and demand written contracts when selling cotton on credit, to avoid losses.

Business Tax Paid in Advance by the Chamber of Commerce - The amount of business tax for the whole year in this county is estimated to be over eight thousand silver dollars. Because the provincial treasury urgently needs funds, the County Chamber of Commerce will pay in advance the amount of two thousand silver dollars for one quarter, and plans to submit a request to the provincial department to start collecting the tax from the autumn to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants.

Wujiang 77

Business Tax Still Levied on Agencies Engaging in Retail - The County Chamber of Commerce of this county previously received approval from the Department of Finance to collect the business tax of the eight districts under the jurisdiction of the County Chamber of Commerce, with a total tax amount of 15,000 silver dollars for the whole year. Because the rice industry requested exemption from the tax, the chamber specially submitted a request to the Department of Finance for clarification. An order from the Department was received yesterday, stating that agents acting as intermediaries for buying and selling should be taxed on this basis; however, those who also engage in retail businesses should still be subject to business tax, and shops selling goods that also sell tobacco and alcohol should still be subject to business tax.

Continuous Heavy Rain Causes City Walls to Collapse - Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been continuous rain and river levels have risen sharply. Yesterday and today, there was even heavier rainfall, and low-lying areas have become inundated. A section of the city wall from the East Gate to the Little East Gate of this city collapsed due to the heavy rain. The Construction Bureau has dispatched personnel to survey the site in order to hire workers for repairs.

Wuxi 78

Submitting a Request for Relief from Room Rent Expenses - In recent years in this county, business has flourished and rents have increased frequently. As a result, landlords near the city area consider their houses to be rare commodities. Therefore, tenants suffer greatly. For this reason, the tenants have organized an association to seek survival. Recently, in front of Qitai Inn on Tongyun Road outside Guangfu Gate, there are four houses that have been rented to Fengtaiyuan, Huadeli, and other companies to conduct business. Last month, the lease period expired. Fengtaiyuan and the other three companies applied to the inn to renew the lease, but the inn used the excuse that the premises were to be taken back for self-use, and demanded an extra fee, which led to negotiations and disputes and fighting at the Public Security Bureau before being transferred to the County Court. Yesterday, Fengtai and other firms formally submitted a request to the County Court for relief in order to maintain their business.

Three Robberies Occur in Rural Areas in One Day - In the 3rd District (Yangming) and the 14th District (Kaihua) under the jurisdiction of this county, three robberies occurred in one day yesterday. The details are as follows: (1) At about 2 a.m. yesterday, more than 30 robbers suddenly came to the house of the late former Jiangsu Provincial Assemblyman Tao Chunzhou near Fangqiao, Kaihua. Each held a handgun and flashlight. They broke down the door and entered. Chunzhou's son, Akang, is doing business in Shanghai, and only women were at home. In terror, they all hid in a dark room. The robbers then searched at will and left only after an hour, having plundered to their satisfaction. The loss was estimated to be about three or four thousand dollars. (2) At the same time, at a certain surname's house in Xutao Lane near the scene of the incident, more than ten robbers suddenly came and broke down the door. The heads of the household were already asleep. They saw that the robbers all had handguns and dared not resist, allowing them to search and plunder at will. The loss was estimated to be several hundred dollars. (3) At the house of a commoner, Lu Afu, at Dasong Fentou, Yangming, four robbers with knives and sticks arrived at the same time, pushed and pried the wall to enter, and locked Lu's wife, Ms. Ma, in a room. They began to search but Lu's family was very poor and they could not find anything. They only obtained a few silver dollars and more than ten cloth garments. All three cases were reported to the county yesterday.

Changzhou 79

Food Grain Management Committee Holds Meeting - The Wuyi Food Grain Management Committee held its first meeting at 3 p.m. on the 23rd at the County Government. Zhang Pengzhu chaired the meeting. Matters discussed: (1) Mutual election of Tu Gongfu, He Naiyang, Guo Cifen, Gao Bozhen, and Bao Zongmou as standing committee members. (2) Mutual election of Tu Gongfu as the head of the General Affairs Section, He Naiyang as the head of the Statistics Section, Bao Zongtang as the head of the Management Section, Gao Bozhen as the head of the Investigation Section, and Guo Cifen as the head of the Transportation Section.

Kidnapping and Robbery Occurs in the Third District - The house of Zhao Meixue in Lanlu Township, Third District, Wuyi County, was suddenly robbed the night before last. After searching and plundering, they kidnapped Zhao Meixue as they were not satisfied with their haul. Afterwards, Zhao's mother reported the kidnapping to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau and sought to rescue her son. On the 23rd, the branch reported the case to the City Public Security Bureau and requested a joint effort to apprehend the perpetrators.

Transfer of Director of the Construction Bureau - Zhuang Zhongxi, Director of the Construction Bureau of Wuyi County, submitted his resignation to the Department. It is now known that the Department of Construction has decided to transfer Zhuang Zhongxi to serve as the Director of the Construction Bureau of Lishui County, and to transfer Xu Jiamo, the original Director of the Construction Bureau of Lishui County, to serve as the Director of the Construction Bureau of Wujin County. The matter will be submitted to the provincial government meeting on the 24th for approval, and orders will then be issued to comply with the arrangements.

Jiangyin 80

County Government Meeting Resolves Important Cases - The county government held its 120th county government meeting on the 20th. County Magistrate Peng presided over the meeting, which resolved important cases: (1) Regarding the current situation of the mold rain disaster, personnel have been sent to the countryside to investigate and report on the serious disaster situation. How should each district quickly raise relief funds? (1) The percentage of damage should be properly planned and reported to the province after the autumn assessment for exemption. (2) The detailed disaster situation should be reported to the Provincial Relief Committee for assistance. (3) The Agricultural Improvement Field should quickly plan timely replanting methods and submit them to the county for promulgation to the disaster-stricken areas. (2) The county government, as well as the Public Security, Construction, Finance, and Education Bureaus, provides a monthly subsidy of 160 silver dollars to Chengqing Daily. Given the current shortage of local funds, the subsidy should be discontinued. (Note: The Chengqing Daily is the official newspaper of the party and government organs, decided by the party and government meeting during the term of the former County Magistrate Li, with the four bureaus of the government providing a monthly subsidy of 160 silver dollars.) Passed as proposed. (3) No official documents of various agencies may be published before they have been signed and issued.

Nantong 81

Disaster Relief after Flooding in Four Townships - Due to incessant rain in the four townships of Nantong, the Yanyun River and the Huaiwei River have risen sharply, causing flooding. The County Government Construction Bureau has opened all the sluices and dams along the Jianghai River and is dredging the Yaowang Port in the Yellow Sea coast to provide relief through labor.

Bandits Dispersed in Tongru Area - A group of bandits was discovered in the Jiuhuashan and Zhengtao areas bordering Nantong, Rugao, and Gaoyou, burning and looting and kidnapping people. The police teams and defense corps of the two counties joined forces to intercept them. The bandits have now retreated by boat from Yong'an Sand. A search is underway in the area for fleeing bandits.

All Sectors Pay Attention to the Water Police Chief Assassination Case - The case of Xie Zezhi, the chief of the stationed Nantong Water Police, being stabbed six times by Yan Zheming, and Yan being shot and killed by police officers in front of the court, is under investigation by the court due to unclear circumstances. The Lawyers' Association is pursuing the matter, and various sectors of the community are paying close attention to the case due to the various rumors circulating.

Yangzhou 82

Prison Warden Escapes after Committing Opium Offense - Chen, the president of Jiangdu County Court, following instructions from the High Court, investigated Cao Yukun, the warden of Jiangdu County, based on a confidential report that he was smoking opium, etc. He dispatched Judge Huang Zhe and clerk Yin Yongxi, along with two police officers, Wu and Zhu, to investigate and found the report to be true. Upon returning to the court, President Chen planned to detain Cao pending instructions from the High Court. It was also learned that Cao had already escaped from the back door. On the same day, when the judge inspected the prison warden's office, he also searched the prison cells by number and found opium paraphernalia in cell number four. The warden's duties are now temporarily assumed by Xu, the captain of the second police squadron under the county magistrate.

Gaoyou 83

A Brief Account of the Flood in Huxi - In the Huxi area under the jurisdiction of this county, including Minjiaqiao, Jia Gou, Huangdangqiao, Ta'erji, and Jingou, there has been a foot of rain in recent days. In addition, the lake water has been increasing daily, causing all the outer embankments near the lake to be submerged, destroying thousands of acres of crops and hundreds of houses. Many people and animals have drowned. Residents are taking their elderly and children and fleeing to the inner embankments. The situation is extremely dire.

Wu's Agency in Xingang Township Robbed - A customer named Gu visited Wu's agency in Xingang Township, District 11 of this county, the day before yesterday to purchase grass and paid 100 yuan in advance. However, at about 1 a.m. that night, six robbers suddenly arrived, each holding a handgun, and broke down the door. They first grabbed the owner of the agency, Wu Guoxing, and burned both of his armpits with candles, forcing him to hand over the money. Unable to bear the pain, Wu handed over the customer's 100 yuan. After obtaining the money, the robbers searched the customer's pockets and took more than 20 yuan. They then entered the bedroom, overturning boxes and cabinets, and stole clothing and other items. The loss is estimated to be about 200 yuan.

Shangyu 84

A Rapid Boat from Yu to Yao is Robbed - The waterway between Shangyu and Yao counties is separated by sixty *li*. There have always been two rapid boats traveling back and forth daily. On the morning of the 22nd, the rapid boat traveling from Yu to Yao, sailing to Yongsibao Bridge, which bordered the two counties, suddenly had two passengers disembark, one of whom carried a rattan suitcase. At the time, the other passengers did not pay much attention. As the boat approached Anwan in Yao territory, the two passengers suddenly stood up, each drawing a handgun to intimidate the passengers and ordered the boatman to stop the boat and moor to the shore. The robbers then searched for the silver and money being transported, which was hidden under the deck of the cabin. At the same time, one robber searched the passengers one by one for silver ornaments, putting them into the rattan suitcase. After completing the robbery, they left two bullets and fled ashore. After checking, none of the twelve passengers were spared, especially a Mr. A who lost several hundred dollars, and a Mr. B who lost a gold chain. The known losses of the boatmen are: 400 silver dollars and 1000 small silver coins entrusted to Chengzhong Xiankang Village, 23 dollars from Hexing Fruit Shop, and over 100 dollars from Heng Hao Sauce Garden. The total losses are estimated to be nearly 1000 dollars. After the incident, the boat immediately returned to Yucheng and reported the incident to the governments of both counties for investigation and arrest.

Ningbo 85

The Intense Anti-Japanese Sentiment of the Public in the Port - All sectors of Yin County held an anti-Japanese movement rally at the public sports ground at 9 a.m. yesterday. More than 2,000 people from various agencies and public groups participated. Wu Wangji chaired the meeting and passed three resolutions: (1) To establish the Yin County National Everlasting Economic Severance Committee against Japan. (2) To send a telegram to the whole country to intensify the anti-Japanese and support-overseas-Chinese work. (3) To inform merchants in the county that they must no longer import Japanese goods. After chanting slogans, the meeting was adjourned. It was originally intended to hold a parade after the meeting, but it was postponed due to rain.

Letter from Anhui Northern Office of the Red Swastika Society 86

Respectfully informing you that this time, the severe floods in northern Anhui have inundated eighteen counties, surrounding thousands of *li*, submerging countless fields and crops, and washing away many houses and livestock. The office has received reports from various branches that are deeply saddened by the situation. Emergency meetings have been held for days to send telegrams to the central government and the provincial government, as well as various charitable organizations, to appeal for help. Currently, the Beijing Red Swastika Society, the Jinan Branch, the Southeast Main Society, the Yantai Branch, the Shanghai Wuhu Datong Branches, and Mr. Su Minsheng and Mr. Jiang Shenxiang have successively remitted relief funds, totaling more than 10,000 yuan. The Anhui Red Swastika Society has rapidly allocated the funds and dispatched personnel to various disaster areas to investigate and distribute emergency aid.会长Zheng Daolin will investigate and distribute aid in Wuhe, Wuqia, Sixian, Jiangba;会长Chen Heng will investigate and distribute aid in Linhuai and Changhuaiwei; Peng Xudan and Sun Wanpin will investigate and distribute aid in Huaiyuan;会长Xu Rankong and Xiao Wancheng will investigate and distribute aid in Fuyang, Yingshang and Zhengyang; Wang Daoyuan will supervise Zhang Huasheng in investigating and distributing aid in 宿xian;会长Li Lingxin and Niu Zhanlu will investigate and distribute aid in Shouxian and Fengtai; and丁Ding Yuanbin and Zhu Xiangwu will investigate and distribute aid in Lingbi. However, the disaster is severe and the funds are limited, making it difficult to provide adequate relief. It is hoped that generous philanthropists from all quarters will continue to provide assistance to rescue the survivors and plan for the aftermath. We are deeply grateful. Hereby informing that the贵报 will record and issue the启示 from the Anhui Northern Office of the World Red Swastika Society, July 21.

Ministry Order to Accept Students from Wuhan Who Have Undergone Screening 87

The Ministry of Education, in view of the fact that the Wuhan area has already held screening examinations for students from unapproved and closed private colleges and above, has issued a special order to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, all national universities and colleges, and schools above the vocational level. This year's screening examinations for graduates and students from unapproved and closed private colleges and above will be held in Wuhan. The Wuhan District Screening Examination Committee for Graduates and Students from Unapproved and Closed Private Colleges and Above has submitted a report on the handling situation and examination results. After detailed review by the Ministry, there are no objections. All qualified and demoted students have been issued transfer certificates separately by the Ministry, ordering them to apply to public and approved private secondary and above schools. In addition to separate distribution, the Ministry orders the said department to forward the order to the provincial and approved private secondary and above schools for compliance. This order.

Anhui Education Compilation 88

▲Distribution of Special Funds for Compulsory Education - The Anhui Education Department previously proposed to the provincial government to use special funds for compulsory education. After the 140th Standing Committee Meeting of the Provincial Government, the Ministry ordered the Education Department to sincerely propose a method for further review. The 141st Standing Committee Meeting has passed the method proposed by the Education Department. The method is roughly as follows: 1. 1,000 yuan per county; 2. After receiving the funds, the education bureaus of each county should store them in a special account; 3. This fund is specifically for purchasing teaching materials needed for the various primary schools in each county; 4. The education bureau should convene a committee for compulsory education to properly allocate the funds, which can only be used after approval by the Department; 5. After the funds are used, receipts must be submitted to the county government for verification and cancellation.

The Enthusiasm for Applying to Two Universities 90

▲Central Political School - Due to the Central Political School's serious management and strict discipline, many high school graduates who aspire to study are applying. The fact that so many people applied to a university of this type breaks the previous records in various places.

▲Wuhan University - A total of 1,289 people have registered to apply for admission to National Wuhan University this year, including 491 in Nanjing, 360 in Shanghai, and 438 at the Wuhan campus. All the freshman exam papers have been carefully evaluated by the school's examination committee. A total of 33 freshmen have been admitted to the Faculty of Arts, 38 to the Faculty of Law, 25 to the Faculty of Science, and 15 to the Faculty of Engineering. 15 applicants to the Faculty of Engineering were admitted to the Faculty of Science. 11 transfer students were admitted to the Faculty of Arts, 9 to the Faculty of Law, and 3 to the Faculty of Science. One applicant for the third grade was admitted to the second grade in the Faculties of Arts and Law. Four applicants for the second grade were admitted to the first grade in the Faculty of Arts, three in the Faculty of Law, and one in the Faculty of Science. A total of 159 students were admitted, including 49 freshmen (47 male, 2 female) and 4 transfer students in Nanjing, 41 freshmen and 7 transfer students in Shanghai, and 36 freshmen (28 male, 8 female) and 22 transfer students (20 male, 2 female) at the Wuhan campus.

Guangzhou Zhongda Adds a Girls' Middle School 92

The Affiliated Middle School of National Zhongshan University in Guangzhou was originally co-educational. After the National Education Conference decided on the principle of separate schools for boys and girls three years ago, the Affiliated Middle School sent the female students to Zhixin Girls' Normal School and other schools due to insufficient school premises. Now, because the Affiliated Primary School has expanded its school buildings with the donation of Feng Pingshan, it has been decided to convert a part of the old school buildings of the Affiliated Primary School into a girls' middle school department. It is reported that all planning for the girls' middle school department will be presided over by Dr. Zhuang Zexuan, the director of the Department of Education and the Research Institute of the school, who will abolish the method of teachers lecturing and students listening, and ringing bells for class, following the latest new education trends, and focus on practical home economics exercises to develop life skills and cultivate reading and independent work habits to develop self-study abilities. The report will begin on July 20th, the preliminary examination on August 15th, and the re-examination on the 20th.

The Liang Huai Middle School Alumni Association Reestablishes its Alma Mater 93

The Standing Committee Members of the Private Liang Huai Middle School Alumni Association, including Wang Zuocai, Song Shenzhi, Yin Gongjian, Guo Shuwen, Xu Junfu, Wan Yixiang, and Yu Yingtian, because the association was formed by merging the alumni associations of Yi Xun Middle School, Liang Huai Middle School, Yangzhou Middle School, and Huaiyang Combined Middle School, first held a meeting to restore Liang Huai Middle School, and submitted a document to the Jiangdu County Government for approval. Preparations have been underway for years, and a beginning has been made. Subsequently, regarding the issue of the school site, another submission stated that the Deputy Transport Commissioner of Huainan had received a letter instructing the county to investigate and allocate the old school buildings. Recently, during the enrollment period, another request was submitted to the Education Bureau, which forwarded it to the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, to first organize a board of directors. Mr. Wang Jingting, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, was elected as the Standing Chairman of the school's board of directors, and the Standing Chairman then appointed Zhang Tongqing, a graduate of Dongda University, as the Principal.

For example, nine medals per item would be exchanged for water and other miscellaneous expenses. Our country did not receive any money. China's participation this time is entirely for research purposes, and to show that our country also has a swimming team organization. It is necessary to gather talents and sell them for resistance, or it will not be able to resist later. Therefore, it is necessary to organize a special team. It is not that Binqi wants fame. Today, I hope that reinforcements will attend, so that they can practice and help in the future to attend the National Games. It is also heard that the person with the most points will be awarded a silver shield by the Shanghai Standard Sports Equipment Company.

The Superior Basketball Skills of Zhonghua Basketball Team Triumph Over Shangda 99

| Thirty-Two to Twenty Points |

▲ Tonight, Shangda Battles Hujiang Middle School Affiliated High School

▲ Shangda's Final Battle in Shanghai

Last night, the basketball team of Chih Chi University defeated the basketball team of Japanese Shangda University by thirty-two to twenty points at the Zhonghua Basketball Team. The audience was the largest in recent days, admiring the deep cultivation of Chih Chi's basketball skills. This was Shangda's fifth defeat.

▲ Strong Resistance: At the beginning of the game, Shangda resisted strongly. After Kong Guangyi scored the first point, the score difference was only one or two points, and there were two ties at five to five and eight to eight. Shangda relied on its rapid passing and often launched attacks. Chih Chi roared, and the whole army advanced fiercely, quickly achieving a great advantage of fifteen to nine, winning the first half with fifteen to eleven.

▲ Smooth Operation: In the second half, Chih Chi gradually became more skilled, and the operation was smooth and unobstructed. They scored eight points in one go, creating a score of twenty to twelve. Seeing the fierce momentum, Shangda defended carefully and adjusted its troops from time to time. Chih Chi's score generally exceeded by seven or eight points. When it reached twenty-five to seventeen, Yang Zhongjiang suddenly withdrew due to four fouls. The military appearance did not move slightly because of this. Qian and Kong, the two forwards, coordinated with each other, winning a big victory of twenty-eight to eighteen, with great cheers. In the end, they won thirty-two to twenty.

▲ Not Yet Satisfied: With Chih Chi's basketball skills, they should have defeated Shangda severely. Yesterday's winning points were still not enough to satisfy our expectations. The reason is that they have not been familiar with the ball for many days, resulting in the loss of many hittable balls. However, the agility of Yang and Qian, the two forwards, and the bravery and composure of Kong, the forward, are still undiminished. For Shangda, Nagai and Kaneko are worth watching.

▲ Shanghai Team to Battle: Today, the Hujiang Middle School Affiliated High School, which dominates the sea, will battle Shangda and should be able to win. The game will still be at the basketball hall at 8 PM. This is Shangda's last battle in Shanghai.

▲ Thirty-five Countries and 2,000 Athletes Will Participate

▲ Fifteen Sports Categories and 135 Events

| Opening on July 30th and Closing on August 14th Next Year |

Los Angeles, July 1st Letter Next year on July 30th, this city will have thirty-five countries and 2,000 male and female athletes, participating in the grand 10th World Games. US President Hoover will personally attend the opening ceremony, showing the importance of the event, and will also tour various venues, viewing the competitions, in order to boost the spirit of the athletes. The Games will have fifteen sports categories, divided into a total of 135 events. The most important track and field competition will be held daily from July 30th to August 7th. Notice on Handling the Jiangsu Provincial People's Amateur Games 103

The Shanghai County Education Bureau received an instruction from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education yesterday, stating that the Ministry of Education issued a general outline for the management of the People's Amateur Games, which was copied and issued by the Bureau under Instruction No. 1012. In order to facilitate the handling of the games by each county, nine items of guidelines for handling the People's Rest Time Games in each county of Jiangsu are specifically formulated. In addition to separate orders, a copy is attached for your reference. Please order the Bureau to follow these instructions and instruct the sports field to follow this order. The nine items of the guidelines are recorded below: (1) In order to arouse the interest of the people in sports and promote the universal development of physical education, each county should hold one or two People's Amateur Games every spring or autumn. (2) The dates for holding the People's Amateur Games in each county may be determined by each county, except for those clearly stipulated by the Provincial Department of Education. (3) The People's Amateur Games in each county should be organized by the Education Bureau in conjunction with sports experts to form a preparatory committee. (4) The People's Amateur Games in each county may stipulate the competition methods and sports events according to local needs and environment. (5) In the People's Amateur Games of each county, except for those who are engaged in sports as a profession and students, all residents living in the local area, regardless of gender and age, may participate. (6) Athletes participating in the People's Amateur Games in each county should go through formal registration procedures. The report form should be printed with detailed information on age, occupation, and address, so that investigation and statistics can be carried out and compared year by year to promote the progress of people's sports. (7) The competition rules used in the People's Amateur Games in each county shall be the standards approved by the National Games and the Chinese National Sports Association in the 20th year of the Republic of China. (8) The People's Amateur Games in each county may prepare various medals and prizes to be awarded to the winners of the competition to encourage them, but the value of the prizes shall not exceed 20 national currency yuan per year. (9) Within half a month after the People's Amateur Games in each county, the handling results (such as the articles of association, the statistics of the age and occupation of the athletes, the competition results, etc.) shall be prepared in duplicate and submitted to the Department of Education for record.

▲ The Subject of the Lecture is Anthropometry

Mr. Jiang Xiangqing has been hired by the Jiangsu Provincial Public Sports Field Service Personnel Summer Training Course and will take a special express train to Zhenjiang this morning to give a short lecture, and will return to Shanghai around the fourth or fifth of next month. The subject of the lecture is anthropometry. Mr. Jiang has a great research on this subject. It is heard that his lecture notes have been pre-ordered by the Benbu Qinfen Bookstore and obtained its copyright, which can be published by the end of September at the latest. It is found that there are few publications in the sports field in our country, and there are even fewer works on sports academic research. The book on anthropometry is even more unprecedented. Mr. Jiang's creation can be said to be the beginning. The association was founded by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education. The students are all guaranteed by the Education Bureaus of each county, with a limit of two people per county. There are more than forty counties that have registered. The lecture period is four weeks, and the lecturers hired are all well-known people in the sports field.

Local News

Heavy Rain Floods the Beijing-Shanghai Railway Tracks Last Night 108

▲ All Trains Temporarily Suspended

▲ The Railway Bureau Finds Ways to Repair

▲ About 300 kilometers of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, between Hepingmen and Yaohuamen stations, was hit by torrential rain and flash floods at about 5:00 PM yesterday. The station platforms were flooded with water, and the tracks were submerged deeply. When the locomotive passed, the train body was submerged. The downward fourth special express train arrived at the place and could not move forward, so it returned to Hepingmen station. The Public Works Department has set about investigating whether the roadbed has been damaged. Therefore, the fourth Beijing-Shanghai special express train, the twenty-sixth Beijing-Xishuangbanna passenger train, the sixth night train, and the night freight train were all suspended temporarily. After the repairs are completed, if there is no heavy rain today, it can be open to traffic within one or two days.

▲ The mountain cave on the east side of Zhenjiang Station was also flooded with water, and the soil on the mountain loosened and fell, so that each train could not move forward. A telegram has been sent to the Zhenjiang Engineering Office to find ways to repair it.

▲ The Chief Engineer of the General Administration, Dexford, and the Chief Section Chief, Chen Zhongying, rushed to the scene of the accident on the night train after hearing the news.

▲ At 1:00 AM this morning (the 25th), a passenger train departed from Xishuangbanna Station and sailed to Shanghai.

The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association is Gradually Seeing Results 109

▲ Merchants Arrive at the Meeting to Request Registration

▲ Chinese Merchant Ships Have Stopped Loading Yesterday

The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association's boycott of Japanese goods movement has gradually seen results after days of active work. The merchants who purchased goods before the 14th have come to the Anti-Japanese Association one after another to receive the form for registration. The details are recorded as follows:

▲ Busy Registration Work Yesterday, the merchants who came to the Anti-Japanese Association to request to receive the form for registration included Yuxing Yarn Shop, Dalu Sock Factory and Huayang Department Store, Jiangsu Match United Association, Brothers Store, Rongchangxiang Foreign Goods Store, Yuanli Cotton Cloth Shop, Jiangnan Paper Mill, Xiangda Foreign Goods Shop, Yifeng Yarn Shop, Zida Cotton Cloth Shop, Taimao Lumber, Hongzhang Textile Yarn Shop, Yongkang Guanghuo Shop, Yuxin Yarn Shop, Daxiang Silk Shop, Yongtaixiang Guanghuo Shop, Huiwentang Printing Bureau, Yuanxiang Hardware Shop, Dechangxiang Guanghuo Shop, Defeng Changlongji Foreign Cloth Shop, Yingfeng Huahang, Dacheng Foreign Goods Shop, Xiedaxiang Foreign Goods Shop, Shunji Foreign Goods Shop, Yutai Paper Shop, Xinrenji Construction Factory, Yexinji Porcelain Cloth Shop, Sanliu Cloth Factory, Yuelai Company, Wei Guozhen, Central Trust Company, Yuchang Steel Essence Factory, Yida Yarn Shop, Jiuji Lumber Company, Yongxin Cloth Factory, Fengtaichang Foreign Goods, Yiyuxing Foreign Goods, Huanan Department Store, Maosheng Yarn Factory, Jin Faxiang Department Store, Tiansheng Yarn Shop, Huada Cloth Factory, Zhonghe Socks, Shixing Cloth Shop, Dafeng Shop, Xintai Cigarette Paper, Tianchengchang Porcelain, Xiangmao South Branch, West Branch, General Branch, Xiacheng Foreign Goods, Shunli Lumber, Gao Baoji Yarn Shop, Shenkang Lumber, Ren Fengji Lumber, Rongxing Yarn Shop, Chen Zhangji Plank Lumber, Qianchang Leather Shop, Yongyu Foreign Goods Shop, Science Instrument Museum, Xiachengxiang, Xiehexing, Dabe Industrial Society, etc., more than 100 companies. Therefore, the registration department's work is extremely busy.

▲ Japanese Goods Arrive Early Shanghai merchants pre-ordered 34,000 pieces of foreign cloth cotton yarn from Japanese merchants. Japan Post increased the number of ships to four to transport the goods scheduled for August in advance. The Tai'an Maru, Yamashiro Maru, and other ships swept the goods from Osaka and Kobe. Yesterday, it was confirmed that the goods had arrived in Shanghai, and it was heard that most of them were purchased by the Changjiang Gang. Japanese merchants are now planning to transfer the goods to Hankou and Yichang.

▲ River Ships Stop Loading Japanese Goods The Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association started inspecting Japanese goods yesterday. Therefore, the Donghuo loaded on the six company river ships a few days ago was very crowded. The day before yesterday was the last day before the inspection. All the Hakka people had to rush out, so the river ships were loaded even more. As of yesterday, the Japanese goods loaded on each river ship were greatly reduced. Chinese merchant ships have begun to refuse to load Japanese goods. British and American river ships do not dare to carry them either. However, Japanese ships still collect and transport goods declared by each Japanese firm. Chinese goods have completely stopped loading on Japanese ships.

▲ Japanese Goods Seized Again Yesterday the Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association seized a large number of Japanese goods at the South Railway Station. Yesterday, they received a secret report stating that a large batch of Japanese cloth would be loaded onto the ship today and transported to the Yangtze River. Therefore, they ordered the inspectors to pay attention. Yesterday afternoon, at the Hongsheng Wharf, two small lighters were found, fully loaded with Dongyang cloth, a total of more than 130 pieces, worth more than 80,000 yuan. After the inspectors interrogated the boatman, they learned that it was declared for export on the Xinningxing Ship, and it was immediately detained. The two ships of goods were escorted by the lighter and driven away from the wharf to report to the General Assembly and ask for instructions on how to deal with it. After the goods were detained, the carrying declaration firm stated to the General Assembly that the goods were declared within the period allowed for export by the General Assembly, and were originally intended to be shipped on the 23rd, but there was no cabin space on each river ship, and they were declared during the allowed transportation period, which is not comparable to those who violate the prohibition order. The General Assembly should forgive the original intention and give it convenience. I don't know if it can be allowed.

▲ The Fish Industry Association Boycotts Goods The Shanghai Fresh Fish, Salted Fish, and Cured Meat Industry Association recently held a joint meeting and decided that from now on, they will unanimously not import Japanese goods, and each industry will organize an economic severance committee to actively handle the boycott of goods movement, and issue a notice to be sent to all stores of the same industry for implementation, and it was also resolved that non-industry cargo customers who privately trade and transport goods to various ports, once found out, all stores of the three industries will permanently sever ties with the customer.

▲ Wuxi Chamber of Commerce Telegram The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce yesterday, saying that Japanese goods in the interior of Jiangsu Province are all imported from Shanghai. If Shanghai can investigate and deduct and eliminate them all, there will be no problems in the interior. The Association should lead the active implementation of this to avoid the import of Japanese goods, which will be of great benefit to the preservation of inland commerce. In addition to the relations with Japan, and actively soliciting aid for overseas Chinese, a separate announcement will be made to all industries. Still awaiting instructions, Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce.

▲ The Export of Canned Sugar Has Increased Greatly After the 24th, the transportation of Dongyang sugar has stopped at each port along the Yangtze River. Each port along the Yangtze River has unanimously switched to buying Hong Kong canned sugar. Yesterday, the first batch of Taikoo canned sugar was transported to Hankou, a total of 6,060 bags, transported by the Huangpu Ship. The Gonghe Ship of Jardine Matheson also transported 3,800 bags.

商会决议对日经济绝交后抵制日货 110

▲成立检查研究两个委员会

▲登记十四日前进货

▲通电全国一致息争对外

上海市商会为了自动对日经济绝交一事，召集临时会员大会，讨论抵制日货办法，到会会员代表极为踊跃，现将详细情形记录如下：

▲到会会员 昨日到会会员，有煤业、南北货业、棉织业、鞋皮订楦业、柴炭业、拍卖业、铜锡业、针织业、潮糖杂货业、南北货拆兑业、航业、绸缎业、鸡鸭行业、船业、丝光棉织业、矿灰厂业、棉布业、碱业、橡皮业、钱业、呢绒业、飞花业、海味业、丝厂业、糖业、纱布业、化妆品业、书业、桂圆业、古玩业、运输业等一百余同业公会代表徐寄廎、严均安、虞洽卿、王延松、诸文绮、王晓籁、陈松源、郑澄清等二百余人。

▲主席报告 主席团公推王晓籁报告开会主旨，大致说，今日临时会员大会，因为自全韩发生排华惨剧后，由上海各界代表大会决议，组织反日援侨委员会，本会也参加工作。但反日援侨，与商界有切肤的关系，因此经常务会议提出由执行委员会决议，商人应该自动奋起，一致对日经济绝交，特召集临时大会，共商反日援侨两种工作，能得到圆满结果。商人同具爱国热忱，应该牺牲处，应当忍痛牺牲，使其持久有效，详细办法，愿意共同讨论。

▲虞氏演辞 虞洽卿起立演说，

大致说，此次抵制日货运动发生后，日纱涨四十两，中国纱涨三四两，各地客商纷纷装运日货，使日货存积者，为之一空，轮船装运，几乎不暇供给，这是由于一般人民，口言爱国，心想发财的缘故。本人认为此次对日经济绝交，是因国家存亡关系，既然属于商人自动自决，即应激发天良，各自努力，务达抵制日货的最后目的云云。

▲讨论各案 主案报告后，即开始讨论。（一）驳运船业同业公会提议，应请大会责成驳运船业同业公会，通告全体会员，随时加以检查案。（二）海味杂货业同业公会提议，抵制日货，以稽查为最难，应请由各业举一识货熟手，组织审查委员会，以免纠纷案。决议，一二两项，并案办理。（一）组织日货检查委员会，由各业推员组织。（二）函复驳船业，拒绝装运日货，并予反日会以合法的便利。（三）棉布业同业公会提议，本埠日厂所制棉布，应请转函反日会，准予照旧通行案。（四）丝光棉织业同业公会提议，对日经济绝交中，应请注意工人生活酌用日纱案。（五）针织业同学业公会提议，国产双股线不敷应用，请妥议善法案。决议，三四五三项，并案办理，根据（一）奢侈品，（二）制成品，（三）必需品，（四）原料，四种原则组织抵制日货研究委员会处理。（六）丝线业同业公会，陈述对日经济绝交意见案。（甲）阅本月十六日大会宣言内开，凡本月十四日进货即须处罚一点，按诸国家法令，应自公布日施行，则十六日以前，商人并未知悉，各同业公会也未奉贵会知照，如何遵行，于法于理，均感窒碍。决议，（子）本月十四号以前被扣货物，由商会请反日会发还。（丑）由各业自动向商会登记后发售，未登记者商会不负责。（寅）登记自本日起，限期二星期。（乙）阅本月二十日报道，反日援侨会公告第二号处置办法。（甲）已定日货者从速退货，设对方不允，如何办理。（乙）（丙）两项，如商号已付守洋者，其损失归何人负担，至于（甲乙丙）三项，设将来发生法律上违约责任归何人担负。决议，交抵制日货研究委员会办理。（丙）用人宜慎重。（丁）办法宜周密。（戊）检查日货或调查日货时，应令货主将货名成色数目，开具详细，点交扣留，点交保管，点交发还，节节缜密，层层负责，审定是否日货，确定扣留放行及详细货物数量，登报披露，决议通过。（八）陆祺生建议，息争御侮四项案，原案计划，为（一）永息内争，（二）防止外侮，（三）地方自卫，（四）尚武精神。决议，登报宣言，通电全国，一致对日。

▲临时提议 （甲）郑缄三提议，前反日会详细账目，应立即公布案。决议 （一）由市商会函反日援侨会转前反日会公布详细账目。（二）组织审查委员会，推举叶容兴、马少荃、陈松源、项松茂、王廉芳、谢仲洛、邵宝兴、郑缄三、郑澄清九人为委员。（乙）虞洽卿提，现在所用的煤，多为日货，国煤不敷应用，应如何办理案。决议，交日货研究委员会办理。（丙）组织筹募救济金分组案。决议，由各业公会，分组办理。议毕，散会。

▲通告各业 该会经临时会员大会决议，自动登记日货后，即发通告说，直接禀告各位，我方已查明此次对日经济绝交，应由商界自动组织，业经本会通电各商会，请他们一致进行，原电已刊登在本市各报纸上，已邀大家阅览，本市为全国所关注，更应首先倡导，以符合自动组织的本旨。兹经本月二十四日本会临时会员大会决议，即日起办理日货登记，凡各公司商号，所进日货，在七月十三日以前的，统应于八月六日以前，自动来本会登记，以便转至反日援侨会，按照将来约定的办法，准许其发卖，所需登记表格，需用者可随时向本会商务科索取，如关于表式填写，有不明白的地方，也可赴该科接洽询问。各商店应知此次对日经济绝交，实为民族争存的最后一道防线，如果从前几次，均能各竭尽血诚，认真办理，那野心家也当稍有顾忌，何至国际惨剧，继续屡次上演，是今日在韩八万华侨的死伤枕籍，流离失所，皆由我商界不能努力争存，以至于召来侮辱开启争端，且商民受辱，本不限于一地一事，如之前济南之役，类似事件皆是突然爆发，我民族不自强，则随时有被人宰割的忧虑，各商家勿以为经商国内，不难达到自身幸免的希望，惟有抱定共同奋斗的宗旨，完成商界的人格，如果迁延观望，竟不履行登记手续，届时如有发生被扣被罚情事，则公义所在，届时各商家，即使想要申诉，本会也难以办理，既失信誉，又遭损害，此中利害，不难两言而决，用特在此诚恳通告，务必望大家查办遵照办理为荷，再者，本会登记日货，与反日会登记日货，同属一事，惟为便利商民起见，故有此项规定办法，此层尤其须注意，专此布告，并颂公众安绥。

▲商会公告 该会又发布即日起开始日货登记公告说，兹经临时会员大会决议，为了实行商界自动对日经济绝交起见，自即日起，办理日货登记，凡本会商家，于七月十三日以前，进有日货者，应于八月六日以前，自动赴本会登记，以便将来按照规定办法，准许其售卖，登记表格，可来会向商务科索取，其填写格式，如未明了，也可向该科接洽询问，倘有未经登记的货，以致被扣被罚者，虽经来会申诉，本会也不便代为办理，务各注意为要，惟希公众鉴察。

各界反日运动 111
